- [Branch](content/animations/graph/node_library/comparison/branch.md): Outputs one of two values based on a boolean condition. This is equivalent to a ternary operator: if Condition is true,...
- [Check Range](content/animations/graph/node_library/comparison/check_range.md): Returns true if Value is between Min and Max (inclusive), false otherwise.
- [Equal](content/animations/graph/node_library/comparison/equal.md): Returns true if A equals B.
- [Greater](content/animations/graph/node_library/comparison/greater.md): Returns true if A is greater than B.
- [Greater Equal](content/animations/graph/node_library/comparison/greater_equal.md): Returns true if A is greater than or equal to B.
- [Animation Graph Node Library](content/animations/graph/node_library/comparison/index.md): Boolean logic gates and value comparison operators for building conditions and branching logic.
- [Less](content/animations/graph/node_library/comparison/less.md): Returns true if A is less than B.
- [Less Equal](content/animations/graph/node_library/comparison/less_equal.md): Returns true if A is less than or equal to B.
- [Nand](content/animations/graph/node_library/comparison/nand.md): Returns true unless both A and B are true (negated And).
- [Nor](content/animations/graph/node_library/comparison/nor.md): Returns true only if both A and B are false (negated Or).
- [Not](content/animations/graph/node_library/comparison/not.md): Inverts a boolean value. Returns true if X is false, and false if X is true.
- [Not Equal](content/animations/graph/node_library/comparison/not_equal.md): Returns true if A does not equal B.
- [Or](content/animations/graph/node_library/comparison/or.md): Returns true if either A or B is true.
- [Xor](content/animations/graph/node_library/comparison/xor.md): Returns true if exactly one of A or B is true.
- [Bool](content/animations/graph/node_library/constant/bool.md): Outputs a constant boolean value.
- [Float](content/animations/graph/node_library/constant/float.md): Outputs a constant floating-point value.
- [Animation Graph Node Library](content/animations/graph/node_library/constant/index.md): Nodes that output a fixed value of a specific type - float, int, bool, vector, quaternion, or matrix.
- [Int](content/animations/graph/node_library/constant/int.md): Outputs a constant integer value.
- [Ivec2](content/animations/graph/node_library/constant/ivec2.md): Outputs a constant 2D integer vector.
- [Ivec3](content/animations/graph/node_library/constant/ivec3.md): Outputs a constant 3D integer vector.
- [Ivec4](content/animations/graph/node_library/constant/ivec4.md): Outputs a constant 4D integer vector.
- [Mat3](content/animations/graph/node_library/constant/mat3.md): Outputs a constant 3x3 matrix.
- [Mat4](content/animations/graph/node_library/constant/mat4.md): Outputs a constant 4x4 matrix.
